 supreme court dwaara niyukt lodha samiti ne guuruuvaar ko bhartiya cricket control board (bisisiai ) ko kaha ki england or wales cricket board (isibi) or bisisiai ke bich ‘prastaavit samjhauta patr’ ‘aadesh kaa hissaa nahin he’ or jab tak vistrut jaankaree nahin muhaiyaa karai jaaegi tab tak bhugtan par koi bhi nirdesh jari nahin kiye ja sakate
 Secretary Ajay Shirke sought instructions from the committee whether he should speak to the ECB to make his payments as the BCCI cannot conduct financial transactions as payments and all arrangements for the visiting team during the bilateral series are made by the domestic board Huh
 iske jawaab main lodha panel ne kaha, ‘bisisiai or isibi ke bich prastaavit samjhauta patr dwipaksheeya cricket niti se sambandhit he jo samiti ke aadesh kaa anivaary hissaa nahin he
 As far as the payments are concerned, if they are given directly by the BCCI, then no instructions can be given by this committee unless the information related to the case is provided by the BCCI
 ’ panel sachiv gopal shankaranarayan dwaara likhe gaye email main kaha gaya, ‘cricket calendar main kisi bhi baadha se bachane ke liye or khel ke premiyon kaa lutf uthaanaa sunishchit karne ke liye bisisiai ko salaah di jaati he ki vah supreme court ke 18 july 2016, saat aktubar 2016 or 21 aktubar 2016 ke aadesh main diye gayi nirdeshon kaa paalan kare
 Comments panel ne adhyaksh anuraag thakur or shirke ko bheje gayi apane patr main yah bhi spasht kiya ki vikritaon or thekedaaron kii na to pahchaan karnaa or na hi unki niyukti samiti ke kaam yaa gatividhiyon main shaamil hai lekin unako ek antim seemaa nirdhaarit kerani hogi
 The panel also directed the BCCI to give all the necessary information regarding appointment of independent auditors and tendering of IPL by 8 November
 samiti ne phir se bisisiai pramukh thakur ko ‘bisisiai kii ore se 21 oktober 2016 ko die gaye supreme court ke aadesh kaa aupchaarikta se paalan karne ke liye apramanit halafanama’ dene kii baat yaad dilaai
 Shirke wanted instructions for appointment of vendors for the international and domestic season, IPL 2017
 (hedline ke alaava, is khabar ko enditivi team ne sampadit nahin kiya he, yah syndicate feed se sidhe prakashit kii gai he
 ) sachiv ajay shirke ne samiti se nirdesh maange the ki kya unhen isibi se apane bhugtan karne ke liye bol dena chahie kyonki bisisiai vittiya lenden nahin kar saktaa kyonki dwipaksheeya siries ke dauraan daura karne vaali team ke liye bhugtan or saare intjamaat gharelu board dwaara hi kiye jate hai
 In response, the Lodha panel said, 'the proposed mou between BCCI and ECB pertains to bilateral cricket policy which is not an essential part of the committee's order
 jahaan tak bhugtan kaa sambandh he, agar ye bisisiai dwaara sidhe diye jate hai to is samiti dwaara tab tak koi nirdesh nahin diye ja sakate hai, jab tak bisisiai dwaara maamle se sambandhit jaankaree muhaiyaa nahin karaayi jaati
 In an email written by panel secretary Gopal Shankaranarayana said, "in order to avoid any obstruction in the cricket calendar and to ensure that the lovers of the game are entertained, the BCCI is advised to submit to the Supreme Court on 18 July 2016, Follow the instructions given in the order of 7 October 2016 and 21 October 2016
 ’ tippaniyan The panel, in its letter to Chairman Anurag Thakur and Shirke, also made it clear that neither the vendors nor contractors are identified nor their appointments are involved in the work or activities of the committee but they must set a final limit
 panel ne bisisiai ko yah bhi nirdesh diya ki vah swatantra auditor kii niyukti or aath november tak ipel kii nivida diye jane ke sambandh main sabhi jaruri soochna de
 The committee again reminded BCCI chief Thakur to give an 'unproven affidavit for formally complying with the Supreme Court order given by BCCI on 21 October 2016'
 shirke antarrashtriya or gharelu satr, ipel 2017 ke liye vikritaon kii niyukti ke liye nirdesh chaahate the
